This line could be vertical, horizontal or diagonal and must consist of at least four chips.\r\n\r\nTo win you must be the first to connect 4 of your color chips in a row either horizontally, vertically, or diagonally!\r\n\r\nFour in a Row is the perfect game to play against friends, or any time you have a few minutes to spare. Each player takes turns choosing a column to drop a chip in. Your goal is always to connect four chips of your own color in a row, either vertically, horizontally or diagonally.
